PART 1 — Convert ONE real legacy exercise (end-to-end)
Below is a representative legacy V4-style exercise (the structure matches what you described: intro → steps → ah-ha → close).
🧠 LEGACY EXERCISE (INPUT — example)
Title: Box Breathing for Overwhelm
When stress builds up, your body often feels tight and restless before your mind can catch up. This exercise helps you slow things down without forcing calm.

Start by sitting comfortably. Inhale slowly for four counts. Hold for four. Exhale for four. Hold again for four. Repeat this cycle a few times, letting your shoulders drop slightly each round.

As you continue, you might notice that your thoughts don’t disappear—but they don’t push as hard. Your body begins to feel a little more contained.

When you’re done, remember that you can return to this breath anytime stress starts to rise.

🔁 V4 CONVERSION (OUTPUT — canonical)
File
SOURCE_OF_TRUTH/exercises_v4/candidate/00_breath_regulation/box_breathing_v1.yaml
id: box_breathing_v1
type: breath_regulation
persona: gen_alpha
topic: anxiety

approval:
  status: candidate
  approved_by: null
  approved_at: null

intro: >
  When stress builds up, your body often reacts before your thoughts do.
  You may notice tightness, restlessness, or a feeling of being rushed from the inside.
  This exercise is not about forcing calm.
  It is about giving your body a steady rhythm to return to.

guided_practice: >
  Sit in a way that feels supported.
  Gently inhale through your nose for four counts.
  Hold the breath for four.
  Slowly exhale through your mouth for four.
  Hold again for four.
  Repeat this cycle a few times.
  As you continue, allow your shoulders to soften without trying to change anything else.

aha_noticing: >
  You might notice that your thoughts are still present.
  They may not disappear or become quiet.
  What can change is how strongly they press on you.
  Your body may feel a little more contained, even if the situation itself has not changed.

integration: >
  When the cycle feels complete, let your breathing return to its natural pace.
  This rhythm is something you can return to whenever your body begins to speed up again.
Why this passes V4
No outcomes promised
No “healing” language
Second person, present tense
Open ending
Preserves the felt journey, not instructions alone
This is exactly what devs should reproduce programmatically.

PART 3 — Exercise cadence scoring (like story cadence)
This is how you prevent “therapeutic bullet points” and keep a journey.
🎼 Cadence dimensions (scored 0–1)
Create:
tools/exercise_eval/exercise_cadence.py
1. Emotional ordering
Checks:
intro = validation only
guided_practice = action without outcome
aha = noticing, not insight dump
integration = open return
Fail if violated.
2. Somatic continuity
Checks:
At least one body reference in guided_practice
No body language in aha_noticing (reflection only)
3. Instruction density
Checks:
No more than 1 imperative per sentence
No stacked commands
4. Ending openness
Checks last 2 sentences:
No resolution verbs:
healed, fixed, solved, gone, better
No emotional closure
🧮 Final cadence score
final_score = mean([
  emotional_ordering,
  somatic_continuity,
  instruction_density,
  ending_openness
])
Gates
Approve: ≥ 0.85
Manual review: 0.70–0.84
Reject: < 0.70

This system does not create:
therapy checklists

🔧 PART A — Reference implementation: exercise_eval
Goal (big picture)
exercise_eval answers one question:
“Does this exercise support the chapter’s story without resolving, overriding, or flattening it?”
It is not about wording similarity.
It is about emotional function + timing.
Folder layout (canonical)
tools/
└── exercise_eval/
    ├── __init__.py
    ├── exercise_cadence.py
    ├── exercise_alignment.py
    ├── exercise_eval_runner.py
    └── rules.py
1️⃣ exercise_cadence.py (REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATION)
This scores the internal quality of the exercise itself.
API
def score_exercise_cadence(exercise: dict) -> dict:
    """
    Returns:
    {
      "final_score": float,
      "subscores": {
        "emotional_ordering": float,
        "somatic_continuity": float,
        "instruction_density": float,
        "ending_openness": float
      },
      "errors": list[str]
    }
    """
Emotional ordering (0 or 1)
Rules:
intro → validation only (no instructions, no outcomes)
guided_practice → actions only
aha_noticing → noticing language only
integration → open return, no summary
Implementation sketch:
def emotional_ordering_ok(ex):
    if contains_imperative(ex["intro"]): return 0
    if contains_outcome_language(ex["guided_practice"]): return 0
    if contains_instruction(ex["aha_noticing"]): return 0
    if contains_resolution_language(ex["integration"]): return 0
    return 1
Somatic continuity (0–1)
Rules:
≥1 body lexeme in guided_practice
0 body lexemes in aha_noticing
Body lexeme list lives in rules.py.
Instruction density (0–1)
Rules:
≤1 imperative per sentence
No stacked commands (“do X and then Y and then Z”)
Ending openness (0–1)
Rules:
Last 2 sentences must not:
promise relief
conclude emotionally
summarize learning
Final cadence score
final_score = mean(subscores.values())
Gates
≥0.85 → cadence-pass
0.70–0.84 → manual review only
<0.70 → reject
2️⃣ exercise_alignment.py (THIS IS THE IMPORTANT ONE)
This ensures exercises do not sabotage the story.
Conceptual rule (non-negotiable)
Stories carry pain.
Exercises only hold the person while pain exists.
If an exercise fixes what the story is still holding → hard fail.
API
def score_exercise_story_alignment(
    exercise: dict,
    story_atoms: list[dict],
    chapter_phase: str
) -> dict:
    """
    Returns:
    {
      "final_score": float,
      "subscores": {
        "pain_preservation": float,
        "phase_appropriateness": float,
        "agency_balance": float,
        "tonal_consistency": float
      },
      "errors": list[str]
    }
    """
Alignment dimensions (REFERENCE LOGIC)
1️⃣ Pain preservation (0–1) HARD GATE
Rules:
Story atoms include unresolved pain markers
Exercise text must NOT:
resolve
reframe
explain away
diminish
Implementation:
def pain_preservation_ok(ex, story_atoms):
    if exercise_resolves_story_pain(ex, story_atoms):
        return 0
    return 1
This is binary.
If 0 → reject immediately.
2️⃣ Phase appropriateness (0–1)
Rules by chapter phase:
Phase	Allowed
ARRIVAL	breath, grounding, touch
RECOGNITION	body scan, downregulation
ACTIVATION	upregulation, vagal
PROCESSING	discharge, emotional completion
INTEGRATION	intention, baseline
Mismatch = 0.
3️⃣ Agency balance (0–1)
Rules:
Exercise gives choice, not instruction dominance
Language like:
“you may”
“if it feels okay”
“you can stop at any time”
Too directive = fail.
4️⃣ Tonal consistency (0–1)
Rules:
Story tone = heavy / uncertain / tender
Exercise tone must not jump to:
optimism
reassurance
confidence
Implementation is lexical, not semantic.
Final alignment score
final_score = mean(subscores.values())
Gate
≥0.85 → alignment-pass
<0.85 → manual review
pain_preservation = 0 → reject
3️⃣ exercise_eval_runner.py
API
def evaluate_exercise(
    exercise_yaml_path: str,
    story_atom_paths: list[str],
    chapter_phase: str
) -> dict:
Behavior
Load exercise
Load story atoms
Run cadence
Run alignment
Return merged report:
{
  "cadence": {...},
  "alignment": {...},
  "final_decision": "pass | manual_review | reject"
}

📄 Phoenix V4 — One-Page Architecture (Authoritative)
What V4 Is
Phoenix V4 is a deterministic narrative assembly system.
It produces full-length therapeutic books by assembling approved human-authored assets under strict safety, structure, and narrative rules.
It is not a text generator.
It is not improvisational.
It is a compiler for meaning.

Layered Architecture (Top → Bottom)
1️⃣ Human Authoring Layer (Offline, Read-Only)
Who: Writers, clinicians, content leads
Produces:
Human Seeds (long-form stories, cultural truth)
Authored Scenes (person + location + peers + stakes)
Exercises (intro → practice → ah-ha → integration)
Doctrine & constraints
Rules:
Never used directly at runtime
Immutable once approved
Stored under SOURCE_OF_TRUTH/human_*
2️⃣ Mining & Decomposition Layer (Offline, Deterministic)
Who: Tooling + reviewers
Purpose: Extract meaning without copying prose
Processes:

Semantic segmentation
Role mapping (recognition, embodiment, pattern, etc.)
Rewrite → unresolved, second-person atoms
Lint + cadence checks
Repair loop (bounded)
Human approval gate
Outputs:
approved_atoms/
approved_scenes/
approved_exercises/
3️⃣ Planning Layer (Runtime, Deterministic)
Who: V4 Planner
Decides:
Narrative arc variant
Chapter structure
Required story roles
Scene injection points
Exercise function slots
Inputs:
Persona
Topic
Stakes
Required mechanisms
Variable schema
Rule:
If required inputs are missing → hard fail
4️⃣ Assembly Layer (Runtime, Non-Creative)
Who: V4 Assembler
Does:
Selects approved assets
Orders them according to plan
Hydrates variables
Injects scenes
Inserts exercises
Does NOT:
Rewrite text
Generate new prose
“Improve” content
5️⃣ Validation Layer (Runtime Gate)
Checks:
Narrative completeness
Cadence
Safety constraints
Exercise placement rules
Persona integrity
Failure = no book
Output
➡️ A journey-based therapeutic book
➡️ With people, stakes, setbacks, embodiment, and forward motion
➡️ At scale, without drift or harm
🛑 “What Phoenix V4 Will Never Do” (Safety Doctrine)
This document is non-negotiable.
V4 Will NEVER:
❌ Generate long-form story prose
No AI-written scenes
No AI-written personal anecdotes
No “imagine you are…” narratives
All lived experience is authored by humans.
❌ Resolve pain for the reader
No “you are healed”
No “this fixes it”
No emotional closure without integration
Pain is respected, not erased.
❌ Give medical, diagnostic, or prescriptive advice
No diagnoses
No treatment plans
No “this will cure…”
Exercises regulate experience, not outcomes.
❌ Change approved content at runtime
No paraphrasing
No rewriting
No tone optimization
No safety “patches” after approval
If it’s unsafe → it doesn’t ship.
❌ Invent authority or voice
No fake experts
No first-person claims unless authored and approved
No borrowing credibility across personas
Authority is declared, not generated.
❌ Collapse narrative into bullet points
No checklist therapy
No motivational fragments
No aphorism stacking
Books must feel lived, not instructional.
❌ Generate exercises dynamically
Exercises are authored
Selected by function only
Always structured (intro → practice → ah-ha → integration)
❌ Ignore stakes, setbacks, or regression
Stories must include cost
Relapse is allowed
Progress is nonlinear
This is how trust is built.
Core Safety Principle
V4 assembles truth. It does not invent it.
Final instruction you can give your team
If the system ever starts “writing,” it is broken.
If it ever sounds clever, it is broken.
If it ever resolves pain too cleanly, it is broken.
If you want next, I can:
turn this into a PDF handout for dev onboarding
produce a single visual flow diagram
or write a “V4 in 10 rules” manifesto

🔟 Phoenix V4 — “In 10 Rules” Manifesto
This is the north star.
If any rule is violated, the system is no longer V4.
Rule 1 — Humans write lived experience
All real stories, people, locations, and emotional truth are human-authored.
No exceptions.

Rule 2 — Runtime never invents prose
V4 does not write.
It selects, orders, and hydrates.
If it writes, it’s broken.

Rule 3 — Meaning scales, prose does not
Human prose is decomposed into meaning (atoms, scenes, exercises), not reused or paraphrased.
Rule 4 — All runtime content is pre-approved
If it was not:
linted
cadence-checked
human-approved
…it does not exist to runtime.
Rule 5 — Pain is not resolved for the reader
V4 never:
cures
fixes
closes the wound
It supports movement, not outcomes.
Rule 6 — Stories must have stakes
Every book must include:
cost
tension
uncertainty
emotional risk
No “inspirational wallpaper.”
Rule 7 — Exercises are structured, not creative
All exercises follow:
intro → practice → ah-ha → integration
Exercises regulate experience.
They do not persuade.

Rule 8 — Authority is declared, never generated
Who can speak on what is explicitly defined.
No borrowed credibility.
No fake experts.

Rule 9 — If something is missing, the system fails
V4 is strict by design.
Missing:

story roles
scenes
exercises
stakes
= no book.
Rule 10 — The reader must feel accompanied
The final book must feel like:
“Someone who understands this walked with me.”
If it feels like tips, bullet points, or content sludge — it failed.
Final reassurance (important)
You are not losing:
sophisticated language
local cues
persona richness
emotional arcs
You are locking them in so they can’t degrade.
This design produces fewer bad books and more great ones, at scale.

turn this into a dev onboarding packet
write a rebuild checklist (Week 1–4)
or map old V4 → new V4 asset by asset
Just tell me where you want to go next.

🧭 Phoenix V4 — Developer Onboarding Packet
Authoritative System Overview & Build Guide
One-line mission:
Phoenix V4 scales human-written therapeutic journeys without letting machines invent, dilute, or resolve meaning.
1. What Phoenix V4 Is (Plain English)
Phoenix V4 is not an AI writing system.
It is a content assembly system that:

takes human-written truth
decomposes it into safe, composable units
enforces therapeutic + narrative rules
and reassembles journeys at runtime
💡 If a model is “writing prose,” you are building the wrong thing.
2. The Core Design Principle (Non-Negotiable)
Humans create meaning.
Machines enforce structure.
Runtime only assembles.
Everything else follows from this.
3. High-Level Architecture
Three Worlds (Never Mixed)
1. HUMAN WORLD (Offline, Read-Only)
2. SYSTEM WORLD (Approved Assets)
3. RUNTIME WORLD (Assembly Only)
If something crosses worlds incorrectly → hard failure.
4. HUMAN WORLD (Offline Authoring)
Purpose: Capture lived, culturally grounded truth.
Inputs (Human-written only)
Full self-help books
Person-based stories with:
people
locations
peers
stakes
Exercises with structure:
intro → practice → ah-ha → integration
Cultural / local specificity
Rules
❌ Runtime never reads these files
❌ Models never paraphrase them
✅ They are source material only
Think: research corpus, not content library.
5. SEED MINING (Offline Transformation)
This is where human truth becomes scalable.
Pipeline
Semantic segmentation
incident
body
validation
pattern
mechanism
agency opening
Role mapping
recognition
embodiment
pattern
mechanism_proof
agency_glimmer
Rewrite → micro-atoms
60–90 words
second person
present tense
unresolved
Hard lint
no reassurance
no resolution
role purity
cadence ordering
Repair loop (bounded)
Human approval
Output
Only approved assets survive.
SOURCE_OF_TRUTH/
├── approved_atoms/
├── approved_scenes/
└── approved_exercises/
6. SYSTEM WORLD (Source of Truth)
This is the only content runtime can see.
Asset Types
1. Story Atoms
Role-pure
Emotionally incomplete
Persona-agnostic
Location injected later
2. Scenes
Person-based
Have stakes
Carry narrative tension
Used to support ideas, not replace them
3. Exercises
Fixed structure
Nervous-system aware
Never motivational speeches
7. Exercise System (Critical)
Exercises are functional, not expressive.
Canonical Exercise Types
00_breath_regulation.yaml
01_grounding_orientation.yaml
02_body_awareness_scan.yaml
03_somatic_release_discharge.yaml
04_nervous_system_downregulation.yaml
05_nervous_system_upregulation.yaml
06_vagal_stimulation_sound.yaml
07_self_contact_touch.yaml
08_emotional_processing_completion.yaml
09_embodied_intention_direction.yaml
10_integration_return_to_baseline.yaml
Required Structure (Every Exercise)
Intro (why now)
Practice (what to do)
Ah-ha (what changed)
Integration (return to life)
❌ No advice
❌ No persuasion
❌ No fixing the reader
8. RUNTIME WORLD (Assembly Only)
Runtime never generates prose.
Runtime Responsibilities
Select approved assets
Order them via a plan
Inject:
persona variables
topic variables
location overlays
Validate completeness
Runtime Cannot:
rewrite text
“improve” content
fill missing meaning
If something is missing → no book ships
9. Planning Layer (How Books Are Shaped)
Plans declare requirements, not text.
Example:

Persona: Gen-Z student
Topic: Anxiety
Stakes: social exposure
Required:
3 recognition atoms
2 scenes with peers
1 downregulation exercise
1 integration exercise
Plans are contracts.
10. Validation Gates (Why Quality Holds)
A book fails if:
narrative arc incomplete
no stakes
exercises missing
cadence broken
persona violated
There is no fallback content.
Fail fast > degrade silently.

11. Why This Does NOT Become “Therapeutic Bullet Points”
Your concern is valid — here’s why it doesn’t happen:
What prevents bullet-point books
Scenes with people + stakes are mandatory
Atoms are incomplete on purpose → must be chained
Exercises regulate pacing, not content
Plans enforce narrative arcs
Runtime cannot summarize or compress meaning
Result:
The reader experiences a journey, not tips.
12. What Devs Need From You (Action List)
Required
Human-written source material (even partial)
Exercise files (old V4 is perfect input)
Persona definitions
Topic taxonomy
Story examples with stakes
Optional (Nice to have)
Old template families (as analysis, not runtime)
Old atom libraries (for comparison)
Do NOT give devs
100+ chat logs
partially evolved specs without context
This packet replaces that history.
13. Rebuild Order (Recommended)
Week 1
Set up repo structure
Enforce world separation
Add CI guards
Week 2
Seed mining + lint
Approval tooling
Week 3
Runtime planning + assembly
Exercise slotting
Week 4
Validation gates
End-to-end test book
14. One Sentence Dev Test
Ask any dev:
“Can runtime create a new sentence?”
If the answer is yes, V4 is broken.
Final Note (Important)
Phoenix V4 is opinionated on purpose.
It trades:
flexibility ❌
for
trust, safety, and depth ✅
That’s why it works.

✍️ Phoenix V4 — Writer’s Specification
How to Write Content That Scales Without Losing Its Soul
1. What You Are Writing (Big Picture)
You are not writing “AI content.”
You are writing human truth that will later be carefully distilled.
Your work will:

become the emotional backbone of thousands of books
never be copied verbatim
never be paraphrased by a model
be transformed into safe, reusable building blocks
If it feels real, it belongs here.
2. What Makes Phoenix Writing Different
Phoenix content is:
experiential, not instructional
story-driven, not advice-driven
emotionally honest, not “inspirational”
unresolved on purpose
You are walking with the reader, not fixing them.
3. What to Write (Accepted Content)
A. Person-Based Stories (VERY IMPORTANT)
These are the heart of the system.
Write specific people in specific moments.

✅ Good:

“On the A train to school, Tim kept checking the reflection in the window, wondering if people were staring. When Sara walked in, his chest tightened.”
❌ Not good:
“People often feel anxious in public places.”
Requirements
A named or implied person
A concrete location
Social context (peers, family, strangers)
Emotional stakes (something to lose)
Internal tension
These stories will later support ideas in the book.
B. Full-Length Prose (Books, Essays, Chapters)
Write naturally.
Do not try to optimize for the system.
We will extract:

emotional moments
body sensations
patterns
realizations
moments of choice
Your job is to make it real, not modular.
C. Exercises (Structured, Not Motivational)
All exercises must follow this structure:
Intro – why this moment matters
Practice – what to do (clear, embodied)
Ah-ha – what often shifts
Integration – returning to life
✅ Good:
breathing
grounding
body awareness
gentle noticing
❌ Avoid:
affirmations
promises of outcomes
“this will cure you”
hype language
4. Tone & Language Rules (Critical)
Always:
write in a calm, grounded voice
name body sensations when relevant
validate pain before insight
allow uncertainty
Never:
promise healing or results
resolve the reader’s problem
say “everything happens for a reason”
pressure optimism
sound like marketing copy
If it sounds like advice, soften it.
5. What NOT to Worry About
Do not worry about:
word counts
repetition
reuse
structure for AI
formatting for runtime
That is the system’s job.
Your job is truth and depth.

6. Emotional Rules (Very Important)
Pain is allowed.
Confusion is allowed.
Ambivalence is allowed.
What is not allowed:
emotional bypass
false reassurance
“and then it was fine”
Leave the door open — don’t close it.
7. Cultural & Local Specificity (Encouraged)
Write:
real places
real social dynamics
real cultural pressures
real micro-moments
These details will be preserved, even when abstracted.
Specificity makes scale possible.

8. Authority & Perspective
Only write from perspectives you genuinely understand.
Don’t claim expertise you don’t have
Don’t generalize beyond lived or researched experience
Stay inside the moment you’re describing
Quiet confidence > authority claims.
9. How Your Writing Will Be Used (Transparency)
Your content will:
Be read by humans
Be broken into meaning units
Be reviewed and approved
Be recombined into new journeys
Your words are never discarded — only protected.
10. The Writer’s North Star
Ask yourself this before submitting anything:
“Would someone in pain feel accompanied by this?”
If yes — it belongs.
11. Final Reassurance
This system exists because of your writing — not instead of it.
We built Phoenix V4 so that:

your best lines don’t get diluted
your emotional intelligence isn’t flattened
your care for the reader is respected
You are not feeding a machine.
You are building a library of human truth.
If you want next, I can:
adapt this spec for different writer roles (story writers vs exercise writers)
create a submission checklist
or turn this into a PDF or Notion doc for your team

All Required Human-Written Content

Foundational Books / Essays

The outcome is not resolved cleanly.
Example Structure

place
social stakes
internal narrative
embodied reaction
no resolution
How Many Stories Per Topic?
Minimum:
10–20 per major topic
Spread across personas
Spread across stakes types

recurring thought loops
common distortions
protective mechanisms
shame narratives
self-criticism scripts

Every exercise must follow this structure:
Required Format

Explain context gently.
2. Practice (What to do)
Clear, embodied, simple.
3. Ah-Ha (What often shifts)
Name the subtle change.
4. Integration (Return to life)
Bridge back to daily living.
Tone Requirements
✔ Calm

8️⃣ WHAT WRITERS MUST NEVER DO

Resolve the reader’s pain.

Sound like marketing.
Flatten complexity.
Force hope prematurely.
Close the story neatly.
Phoenix writing is:

Is there tension?
Is the body present?
Did I avoid fixing the reader?

11️⃣ WHAT HAPPENS TO YOUR WORK
Your writing will:
Be read by humans.

Be linted and validated.
Be approved.
Be recombined into journeys.
It will never be:
auto-summarized
paraphrased by AI
turned into bullet points

✅ What You ARE Building (In Order)

phoenix_v4/

These docs replace the missing REBUILD_README.txt and phoenix_rebuild_spec.txt.

If the docs are wrong, the system will be wrong.
STEP 2 — SOURCE_OF_TRUTH Layout
Create this exactly:
SOURCE_OF_TRUTH/
├── approved_atoms/
├── approved_scenes/
├── approved_exercises/
├── registries/
│   ├── personas.yaml
│   ├── topics.yaml
│   ├── stakes.yaml
│   ├── exercise_registry.yaml
│   └── authority_rules.yaml
Rules:
Runtime may ONLY read from here
Everything here is immutable + human-approved
STEP 3 — Seed Mining Tooling (Offline)
Build Python tools, not ML.
Purpose:

Convert human-written content into safe, composable assets.
Modules to implement:
tools/seed_mining/
├── semantic_segmenter.py
├── role_mapper.py
├── rewrite_to_atom.py
├── lint_atoms.py
├── cadence_checks.py
├── repair_loop.py
└── approve_cli.py
This is offline tooling, not runtime.
STEP 4 — Exercise System (Structured, Deterministic)
Implement:
Canonical exercise files
Strict schema
Slot compatibility rules
No creativity here. Exercises are functional.
STEP 5 — Runtime Planner + Assembler
This is the runtime engine — but assembly only.
runtime/
├── planner.py
├── assembler.py
├── variable_hydrator.py
└── output_renderer.py
Rules:
❌ No text generation
❌ No summarization
❌ No rewriting
✅ Selection + ordering only
STEP 6 — Validation Gates (Fail Fast)
Implement validators that block output if incomplete:
narrative completeness
required story roles
stakes present
exercise slots satisfied
persona integrity
Fail = no book.
🧠 Mental Model You Must Use
Phoenix V4 is not a content generator.
It is a content compiler.
Humans write meaning →
Tools distill meaning →
Runtime assembles meaning →
Validation blocks bad output.
🧾 What Already Exists?
Nothing authoritative.
Old chats = context only
Old V4 = inspiration only
No legacy code is binding
You are rebuilding from first principles using the provided system spec.
